name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Themed Room (Double bed)
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 7, 2021
msg:Location traffic:
This is the second time I have come. You can find it easily by following the navigation. The hotel is very close to the beach, especially suitable for bringing children, and has its own exclusive beach, which is finer than other places, except for some small shells. There are basically no stones. I don't stick my bare feet.

Room facilities:
The little yellow duck parent-child room we ordered this time has slides and swings. The swings are suitable for very young children. In fact, I basically play on the beach. There is no need to book a parent-child room. I personally feel that it is more appropriate to book a suite at this price. I like to live in a large room comfortably.

food:
Breakfast starts at half past six, and there are not too many people before eight. The breakfast is not rich but the taste is good, and the dishes are served in a timely manner.
You can choose from nearby restaurants for lunch and dinner. Three fisherman steamed seafood are recommended. They are expensive but delicious. There are also many seafood restaurants nearby. You can read the reviews and choose. The seafood dumplings that have been eaten for three days in a row are quite enjoyable.

play:
